ACTOR LShotgunGuy replaces Shotgunguy
{
	Game Doom
	Health 30
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 100
	Speed 8
	PainChance 170
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	SeeSound "shotguy/sight"
	AttackSound "shotguy/attack"
	PainSound "shotguy/pain"
	DeathSound "shotguy/death"
	ActiveSound "shotguy/active"
	Obituary "$OB_SHOTGUY"
	DropItem "Shotgun"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 1, "CS1CS2")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 6, "EP1EP2")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")
	SpawDDS: //(DDS = Drop Down State)
		SPOS AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	CS1CS2:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CS2ShotgunGuy", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	EP1EP2:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Epic1A11", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	AA1:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AAA31", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	See:
		SPOS AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		SPOS E 10 A_FaceTarget
		SPOS F 10 BRIGHT A_SposAttackUseAtkSound
		SPOS E 10
		Goto See
	Pain:
		SPOS G 3
		SPOS G 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		SPOS H 5
		SPOS I 5 A_Scream
		SPOS J 5 A_NoBlocking
		SPOS K 5
		SPOS L -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		SPOS M 5
		SPOS N 5 A_XScream
		SPOS O 5 A_NoBlocking
		SPOS PQRST 5
		SPOS U -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		SPOS L 5
		SPOS KJIH 5
		Goto See
	}
}





ACTOR LChaingunGuy replaces Chaingunguy
{
	Game Doom
	Health 70
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 100
	Speed 8
	PainChance 170
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	SeeSound "chainguy/sight"
	PainSound "chainguy/pain"
	DeathSound "chainguy/death"
	ActiveSound "chainguy/active"
	AttackSound "chainguy/attack"
	Obituary "$OB_CHAINGUY"
	Dropitem "Chaingun"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 1, "CS1CS2")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 6, "EP1EP2")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")
	SpawdDDS:
		CPOS AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	CS1CS2:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CS2ChaingunGuy", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	EP1EP2:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Epic1A9", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	AA1:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AAA30", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	See:
		CPOS AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		CPOS E 10 A_FaceTarget
		CPOS FE 4 BRIGHT A_CPosAttack
		CPOS F 1 A_CPosRefire
		Goto Missile+1
	Pain:
		CPOS G 3
		CPOS G 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		CPOS H 5
		CPOS I 5 A_Scream
		CPOS J 5 A_NoBlocking
		CPOS KLM 5
		CPOS N -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		CPOS O 5 
		CPOS P 5 A_XScream
		CPOS Q 5 A_NoBlocking
		CPOS RS 5
		CPOS T -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		CPOS N 5
		CPOS MLKJIH 5
		Goto See
	}
}



//Arbitrary state keeps this actor alive, when the new monster is spawned this actor is set as master, when the child is destroyed it will destroy this master, which will trigger mapspecials. This must be done for all mapspecial monsters.
Actor Mapspecial : Inventory
{
inventory.maxamount 2
}

ACTOR LBaronOfHell replaces BaronOfHell
{
	Game Doom
	Health 1000
	Radius 24
	Height 64
	Mass 1000
	Speed 8
	PainChance 50
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	+BOSSDEATH
	SeeSound "baron/sight"
	PainSound "baron/pain"
	DeathSound "baron/death"
	ActiveSound "baron/active"
	Obituary "$OB_BARON"
	HitObituary "$OB_BARONHIT"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 5, "VAL")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 8, "SD6SD7")
	SpawnDDS:
		BOSS AB 10 A_Look 
		Loop
	VAL:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Mapspecial",2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Noblocking
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ValiantSuperMancubus", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    Goto Arbitrary
	AA1:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Mapspecial",2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Noblocking
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AAA22", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    Goto Arbitrary
	SD6SD7:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Mapspecial",2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Noblocking
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SD20x6A4", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    Goto Arbitrary
    Arbitrary:
    TNT1 A 1
    Loop
	See:
		BOSS AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Melee:
	Missile:
		BOSS EF 8 A_FaceTarget
		BOSS G 8 A_BruisAttack
		Goto See
	Pain:
		BOSS H  2
		BOSS H  2 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
    TNT1 A 0
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Mapspecial",1,"SpecialDeath")
		BOSS I  8
		BOSS J  8 A_Scream
		BOSS K  8
		BOSS L  8 A_NoBlocking
		BOSS MN 8
		TNT1 AAA 0
		BOSS O -1 A_BossDeath   
		Stop
	Raise:
		BOSS O 8
		BOSS NMLKJI  8
		Goto See
	SpecialDeath:
    TNT1 A 1 A_BossDeath
    Stop
	}
}



ACTOR LZombieMan replaces Zombieman
{
	Game Doom
	Health 20
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 8
	PainChance 200
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	SeeSound "grunt/sight"
	AttackSound "grunt/attack"
	PainSound "grunt/pain"
	DeathSound "grunt/death"
	ActiveSound "grunt/active"
	Obituary "$OB_ZOMBIE"
	DropItem "Clip"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 1, "CS1CS2")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 6, "EP1EP2")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")
	SpawnDDS:
		POSS AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	CS1CS2:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("CS2ZombieMan", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	EP1EP2:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Epic1A8", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	AA1:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AAA32", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	See:
		POSS AABBCCDD 4 A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		POSS E 10 A_FaceTarget
		POSS F 8 A_PosAttack
		POSS E 8
		Goto See
	Pain:
		POSS G 3
		POSS G 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		POSS H 5
		POSS I 5 A_Scream
		POSS J 5 A_NoBlocking
		POSS K 5
		POSS L -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		POSS M 5
		POSS N 5 A_XScream
		POSS O 5 A_NoBlocking
		POSS PQRST 5
		POSS U -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		POSS K 5
		POSS JIH 5
		Goto See
	}
}


ACTOR LDoomImp replaces Doomimp
{
	Game Doom
	Health 60
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 100
	Speed 8
	PainChance 200
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	
	SeeSound "imp/sight"
	PainSound "imp/pain"
	DeathSound "imp/death"
	ActiveSound "imp/active"
	HitObituary "$OB_IMPHIT"
	Obituary "$OB_IMP"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 5, "VAL")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 6, "EP1EP2")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")
	SpawnDDS:
		TROO AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	VAL:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ValiantImp", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	EP1EP2:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Epic2A36", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	AA1:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AAA29", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	See:
		TROO AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Melee:
	Missile:
		TROO EF 8 A_FaceTarget
		TROO G 6 A_TroopAttack 
		Goto See
	Pain:
		TROO H 2
		TROO H 2 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TROO I 8
		TROO J 8 A_Scream
		TROO K 6
		TROO L 6 A_NoBlocking
		TROO M -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		TROO N 5
		TROO O 5 A_XScream
		TROO P 5
		TROO Q 5 A_NoBlocking
		TROO RST 5
		TROO U -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		TROO MLKJI 8
		Goto See
	}
}


ACTOR LArachnotron replaces Arachnotron
{
	Game Doom
	Health 500
	Radius 64
	Height 64
	Mass 600
	Speed 12
	PainChance 128
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	+BOSSDEATH
	SeeSound "baby/sight"
	PainSound "baby/pain"
	DeathSound "baby/death"
	ActiveSound "baby/active"
	Obituary "$OB_BABY"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 5, "VAL")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")
	SpawnDDS:
		BSPI AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	VAL:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Mapspecial",2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Noblocking
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ValiantArachnotron", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    Goto Arbitrary
	AA1:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Mapspecial",2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Noblocking
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AAA120", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    Goto Arbitrary
    Arbitrary:
    TNT1 A 1
    Loop
	See:
		BSPI A 20
		BSPI A 3 A_BabyMetal
		BSPI ABBCC 3 A_Chase
		BSPI D 3 A_BabyMetal
		BSPI DEEFF 3 A_Chase
		Goto See+1
	Missile:
		BSPI A 20 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
		BSPI G 4 BRIGHT A_BspiAttack
		BSPI H 4 BRIGHT
		BSPI H 1 BRIGHT A_SpidRefire
		Goto Missile+1
	Pain:
		BSPI I 3
		BSPI I 3 A_Pain
		Goto See+1
	Death:
    TNT1 A 0
    TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Mapspecial",1,"SpecialDeath")
		BSPI J 20 A_Scream
		BSPI K 7 A_NoBlocking
		BSPI LMNO 7
		TNT1 AAA 0
		BSPI P -1 A_BossDeath
		Stop
    Raise:
		BSPI P 5
		BSPI ONMLKJ 5
		Goto See+1
	SpecialDeath:
    TNT1 A 1 A_BossDeath
    Stop
	}
}



ACTOR LSpiderMastermind replaces Spidermastermind
{
	Game Doom
	Health 3000
	Radius 128
	Height 100
	Mass 1000
	Speed 12
	PainChance 40
	Monster
	MinMissileChance 160
	+BOSS
	+MISSILEMORE
	+FLOORCLIP
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+DONTMORPH
	+BOSSDEATH

	AttackSound "spider/attack"
	PainSound "spider/pain"
	DeathSound "spider/death"
	ActiveSound "spider/active"
	Obituary "$OB_SPIDER"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 5, "VAL")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")
	SpawnDDS:
		SPID AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	VAL:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Mapspecial",2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Noblocking
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ValiantCybruiser", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    Goto Arbitrary
	AA1:
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Mapspecial",2)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Noblocking
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AAA15", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    Goto Arbitrary
    Arbitrary:
    TNT1 A 1
    Loop
	See:
		SPID A 3 A_Metal
		SPID ABB 3 A_Chase
		SPID C 3 A_Metal
		SPID CDD 3 A_Chase
		SPID E 3 A_Metal
		SPID EFF 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		SPID A 20 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget

		SPID J 20 A_Scream
		SPID K 10 A_NoBlocking
		SPID LMNOPQR 10
		SPID S 30
		TNT1 AAA 0
		SPID S -1 A_BossDeath    
		Stop
	SpecialDeath:
    TNT1 A 1 A_BossDeath
    Stop
	}
}


ACTOR LDemon replaces Demon
{
	Game Doom

	PainChance 180

	Height 56

	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP

	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 5, "VAL")
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")

		SARG AB 10 A_Look
		Loop

    stop
	See:
		SARG AABBCCDD 2 Fast A_Chase
		Loop

		SARG G 8 Fast A_SargAttack
		Goto See

		SARG H 2 Fast A_Pain
		Goto See

		SARG J 8 A_Scream

	{

	Goto SpawnDDS
	VAL:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ValiantSpectre", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	
	}
}


ACTOR LCacodemon replaces Cacodemon
{
	Game Doom
	Health 400
	Radius 31
	Height 56
	Mass 400
	Speed 8
	PainChance 128
	Monster
	+FLOAT +NOGRAVITY
	SeeSound "caco/sight"
	PainSound "caco/pain"
	DeathSound "caco/death"
	ActiveSound "caco/active"
	Obituary "$OB_CACO"
	HitObituary "$OB_CACOHIT"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 a_jumpif(CallACS("Maniac") == 7, "AA1")
		HEAD A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	AA1:
    TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("AAA27", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
    stop
	See:
		HEAD A 3 A_Chase
		Loop
	Missile:
		HEAD B 5 A_FaceTarget
		HEAD C 5 A_FaceTarget
		HEAD D 5 BRIGHT A_HeadAttack
		Goto See
	Pain:
		HEAD E 3
		HEAD E 3 A_Pain
		HEAD F 6
		Goto See
	Death:
		// [BB] In ST A_NoBlocking is called in the beginning of the death state.
		HEAD G 8 A_NoBlocking
		HEAD H 8 A_Scream
		HEAD I 8
		HEAD J 8
		HEAD K 8
		HEAD L -1 A_SetFloorClip
		Stop
	Raise:
		HEAD L 8 A_UnSetFloorClip
		HEAD KJIHG 8
		Goto See
	}
}


ACTOR LRevenant replaces Revenant
{
	Game Doom
	Health 300
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 10
	PainChance 100
	Monster
	MeleeThreshold 196
	+MISSILEMORE 
	+FLOORCLIP
	SeeSound "skeleton/sight"

	See:
		SKEL AABBCCDDEEFF 2 A_Chase
		Loop

		SKEL L 5 A_Pain
		Goto See

		SKEL N 7 A_Scream
		SKEL O 7 A_NoBlocking
		SKEL P 7
		SKEL Q -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		SKEL Q 5
		SKEL PONML 5
		Goto See
	}

		SSWV G 4 BRIGHT A_CPosAttack
		SSWV F 1 A_CPosRefire
		Goto Missile+1
	Pain:
		SSWV H 3
		SSWV H 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		SSWV I 5
		SSWV J 5 A_Scream
		SSWV K 5 A_NoBlocking
		SSWV L 5
		SSWV M -1
		Stop
	XDeath:
		SSWV N 5 
		SSWV O 5 A_XScream
		SSWV P 5 A_NoBlocking
		SSWV QRSTU 5
		SSWV V -1
		Stop
	Raise:
		SSWV M 5
		SSWV LKJI 5
		Goto See 
	}
}

ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Spawner
{
    +NOINTERACTION
    +CLIENTSIDEONLY
    States
    {
        Spawn:
        TNT1 A 0
        TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256, "Red", "Green", "Blue", "Cyan", "Yellow", "Magenta", "Multi", "Multi", "Multi") 
        Stop
        
        Red:
            TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Red")
            stop
            
        Green:
            TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Green")
            stop
            
        Blue:
            TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Blue")
            stop
            
        Cyan:
            TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Cyan")
            stop
            
        Yellow:
            TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Yellow")
            stop
            
        Magenta:
            TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Magenta")
            stop
            
        Multi:
            TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Multi")
            stop        
    }
}

ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Red
{
    Translation "192:207=168:191"
    +NOINTERACTION
    +CLIENTSIDEONLY
    RenderStyle "Add"
    var int user_time;
    var int user_shota;
    var int user_shotp;
    var int user_shotx;
    var int user_shoty;
    var int user_shotz;
    var int user_shots;
    var int user_shotcount;
    var int user_shotmax;
    States
    {
        Spawn:
            FWRK A 0
            FWRK A 0 ThrustThingZ(0, random(150, 200), 0, 0)
        
        Run:
            FWRK A 1 Bright A_SetUserVar("user_time", user_time+1)
            FWRK A 0 A_JumpIf(user_time > 30, "Explode_Prep")
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Trail", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
            Loop
        
        Explode_Prep:
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shots", random(5, 10))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotmax", random(10, 30))
            FWRK A 0 A_PlaySound("firework", 0, 1.0, false, ATTN_NONE)
        
        Explode:
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotcount", user_shotcount+1)
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shota", random(0, 359))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotp", random(0, 359))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotx", (cos(user_shota)*user_shots)*cos(user_shotp))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shoty", (sin(user_shota)*user_shots)*cos(user_shotp))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotz", sin(user_shotp)*user_shots)
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Particle", 0, 0, 0, user_shotx, user_shoty, user_shotz, 0, SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
            FWRK A 0 A_JumpIf(user_shotcount > user_shotmax, "Death")
            loop
        
        Death:
            TNT1 A 0
            stop
    }
}

ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Green : Lexicon_Firework_Red     { Translation "192:207=112:127" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Blue : Lexicon_Firework_Red      { Translation "192:207=192:207" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Cyan : Lexicon_Firework_Red      { Translation "192:207=208:223" } // i didnt think this one through(this is actually orange)
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Yellow : Lexicon_Firework_Red    { Translation "192:207=160:167" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Magenta : Lexicon_Firework_Red   { Translation "192:207=250:254" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Multi : Lexicon_Firework_Red     
{ 
    Translation "192:207=80:111"
    States
    {
        Spawn:
            FWRK A 0
            FWRK A 0 ThrustThingZ(0, random(150, 200), 0, 0)
        
        Run:
            FWRK A 1 Bright A_SetUserVar("user_time", user_time+1)
            FWRK A 0 A_JumpIf(user_time > 30, "Explode_Prep")
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Trail", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION)
            Loop
        
        Explode_Prep:
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shots", random(5, 10))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotmax", random(10, 30))
            FWRK A 0 A_PlaySound("firework", 0, 1.0, false, ATTN_NONE)
            
        Explode:
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotcount", user_shotcount+1)
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shota", random(0, 359))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotp", random(0, 359))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotx", (cos(user_shota)*user_shots)*cos(user_shotp))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shoty", (sin(user_shota)*user_shots)*cos(user_shotp))
            FWRK A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_shotz", sin(user_shotp)*user_shots)
            FWRK A 0 A_Jump(256, "Red", "Green", "Blue", "Cyan", "Yellow", "Magenta")
            
        Red:
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Red", 0, 0, 0, user_shotx, user_shoty, user_shotz, 0)
            goto Explode_Cont
            
        Green:
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Green", 0, 0, 0, user_shotx, user_shoty, user_shotz, 0)
            goto Explode_Cont
            
        Blue:
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Blue", 0, 0, 0, user_shotx, user_shoty, user_shotz, 0)
            goto Explode_Cont
            
        Cyan:
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Cyan", 0, 0, 0, user_shotx, user_shoty, user_shotz, 0)
            goto Explode_Cont
            
        Yellow:
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Yellow", 0, 0, 0, user_shotx, user_shoty, user_shotz, 0)
            goto Explode_Cont
            
        Magenta:
            FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Magenta", 0, 0, 0, user_shotx, user_shoty, user_shotz, 0)

        Explode_Cont:
            FWRK A 0 A_JumpIf(user_shotcount > user_shotmax, "Death")
            goto Explode
    }
}

ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Particle
{
    -NOGRAVITY
    +LOWGRAVITY
    +CLIENTSIDEONLY
    RenderStyle "Add"
    States
    {
        Spawn:
        FWRK A 0
        
        Run:
        FWRK A 1 Bright A_FadeOut(0.02)
        FWRK A 0 A_SetScale(scalex-0.02, scaley-0.02)
        FWRK A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Lexicon_Firework_Trail", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_TRANSFERTRANSLATION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE)
        Loop
    }
}

ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Red : Lexicon_Firework_Particle       { Translation "192:207=112:127" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Green : Lexicon_Firework_Particle     { Translation "192:207=192:107" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Blue : Lexicon_Firework_Particle      { Translation "192:207=192:207" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Cyan : Lexicon_Firework_Particle      { Translation "192:207=208:223" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Yellow : Lexicon_Firework_Particle    { Translation "192:207=160:167" }
ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Particle_Magenta : Lexicon_Firework_Particle   { Translation "192:207=250:254" }

ACTOR Lexicon_Firework_Trail
{
    scale 0.4
    +NOGRAVITY
    +CLIENTSIDEONLY
    RenderStyle "Add"
    States
    {
        Spawn:
        FWRK A 0
        
        Run:
        FWRK A 1 Bright A_FadeOut(0.02)
        FWRK A 0 A_JumpIf(scalex > 0.0, "Scaledown")
        loop
        
        ScaleDown:
        FWRK A 0 A_SetScale(scalex-0.01, scaley-0.01)
        goto run
    }
}



ACTOR Lexicon_VoteGun : DoomWeapon
{
  Weapon.SelectionOrder 1
  Weapon.AmmoUse 0
  Weapon.AmmoGive 0
  Weapon.AmmoType ""
  Weapon.SlotNumber 0
  Weapon.SlotPriority 0
  Obituary ""
  Inventory.Pickupmessage ""
  Tag "VoteGun"
  States
  {
  Ready:
    VOTE A 1 A_WeaponReady
    Loop
  Deselect:
    VOTE A 1 A_Lower
    Loop
  Select:
    VOTE A 1 A_Raise
    Loop
  Fire:
    VOTE A 0 A_Playsound("voteshot")
    VOTE A 0 A_SetBlend("FF FF FF", 0.3, 1)
    VOTE A 10 A_RailAttack(0, 7, false, "none", "none", RGF_SILENT, 0, "BulletPuff", 0, 0, 1024.0, 70, 0.5, 0.5)
    VOTE A 0 A_ReFire
    Goto Ready
  Spawn:
    TNT1 A -1
    Stop
  }
}

  }

{

  Radius 16

  Scale 0.8
  Translation "16:39=96:111", "40:47=5:8", "176:191=0:2", "48:71=96:111",
  "72:79=5:8", "128:135=96:111", "136:143=5:8", "144:147=96:111", "148:151=5:8",
  "160:163=96:111", "164:167=5:8", "236:239=5:8", "232:235=5:8", "13:15=10:12"

  {
    Spawn:

    Loop
	See:
    SKEL A 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)
    SKEL A 1 A_Chase
    SKEL B 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)

    SKEL F 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)
    SKEL F 1 A_Chase
    SKEL A 0 A_Jump(32,"Hold")
    SKEL A 0
    Loop
    Wander:
    SKEL A 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)
    SKEL A 1 A_Wander
    SKEL B 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)
    SKEL B 1 A_Wander
    SKEL C 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)
    SKEL C 1 A_Wander
    SKEL D 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)
    SKEL D 1 A_Wander
    SKEL E 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)
    SKEL E 1 A_Wander
    SKEL F 0 A_Recoil(-0.5)
    SKEL F 1 A_Wander
    SKEL F 0 A_Jump(240,2)
    SKEL F 0 A_Look
  	SKEL F 0 A_Jump(64,"Stand") 
    Loop
    Stand:
    SKEL A 0 A_Jump(240,2)
    SKEL A 10 A_Look  
    SKEL A 10
  	SKEL A 0 A_Jump(64,"Wander")    
	Loop
    Hold:
    SKEL A 10 A_Jump(248,2)	
    SKEL A 10 A_Look
    SKEL A 10
    SKEL A 10 A_Jump(2,"Wander")	
    Loop
    Missile: 
      SKEL G 0 A_Jumpifcloser(256, 1)
      Goto See
	  SKEL G 0 A_PlaySound("skeleton/sight")
      SKEL G 3 A_FaceTarget 
      SKEL H 6 A_SkullAttack 
      SKEL I 3 A_Gravity
      Goto See 
    Melee:
      SKEL G 0 A_Jump(16,"Wander")	
      SKEL G 1 A_FaceTarget
      SKEL G 0 A_Recoil(-4.0)
      SKEL G 4 A_SkelWhoosh
      SKEL H 4 A_FaceTarget
      SKEL I 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(1,8)*8,"skeleton/melee","none")
      SKEL I 0 A_Jump(64,"Wander")	
    Goto See
  Pain:
    SKEL L 0 A_ChangeFlag ("NOPAIN", 1)
    SKEL L 1
    SKEL L 0 A_ChangeFlag ("NOPAIN", 0)
    SKEL L 0 A_Jump(96,"Wander")
    SKEL L 3 A_Pain
    SKEL L 0 A_Jump(96,"Wander")
    Goto See
  Death:
    SKEL L 7 A_Pain
	SKEL M 2 A_Scream
    SKEL N 2 A_NoBlocking
    SKEL O 2 
    SKEL P 2
    SKEL Q -1
    Stop
  Raise:
    TNT1 A 0 
    TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag ("NOPAIN", 1)
    SKEL QPONML 5
    TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag ("NOPAIN", 0)
    goto See
	}
}

ACTOR TAT__PracticeTargets  : ZombieMan 32510
{ 
//$Category Monsters
  Speed 8
  Health 150000
  GibHealth -10000
  PainChance 255
  Mass 50
  DropItem "RedCard"
states
  {
  Spawn:
    CPOS AB 10 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    CPOS A 0 A_Recoil(-1)
    CPOS A 1 A_Wander
    CPOS B 0 A_Recoil(-1)
    CPOS B 1 A_Wander
    CPOS C 0 A_Recoil(-1)
    CPOS C 1 A_Wander
    CPOS D 0 A_Recoil(-1)
    CPOS D 1 A_Wander
	Loop
   Pain:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TAT__DeadZombie",0,0,0,Random(-8,8),Random(-8,8),Random(0,16))
	TNT1 A 1
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_Wander
    Goto See
   Pain.TkExplosion:
    TNT1 A 1 Thing_Damage(0,200000)  
    Goto See
   Death:
    CPOS H 5
    CPOS I 5 A_Scream
    CPOS J 5 A_NoBlocking
    CPOS KLM 5
    CPOS N -1
    Stop
   XDeath:
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TAT__GibZombie",0,0,0,Random(-16,16),Random(-16,16),Random(0,32))   
    CPOS O 5
    CPOS P 5 A_XScream
    CPOS Q 5 A_NoBlocking
    CPOS RS 5
    CPOS T -1
    Stop
   Raise:
    CPOS N 5
    CPOS MLKJIH 5
    Goto See
  }
}

ACTOR TAT__DeadZombie
{ 
  Gravity 1.25
  +NoTeleport
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  Radius 20
  Height 16
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    CPOS G 0
    CPOS G 1 A_PlaySound("grunt/death")   
	CPOS HIJKLM 3 Bright
	CPOS NNNNNNNNNN 2 A_FadeOut(0.05) 
	CPOS NNNNNNNNNN 2 A_FadeOut(0.05) 
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR TAT__GibZombie : TAT__DeadZombie
{ 
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    CPOS G 0
    CPOS G 1 A_PlaySound("misc/gibbed")
    CPOS OPQRS 3
	CPOS TTTTTTTTTT 2 A_FadeOut(0.05) 
	CPOS TTTTTTTTTT 2 A_FadeOut(0.05) 
    Stop
  }
}


ACTOR TAT__TkBarrel : ExplosiveBarrel 32511
{ 
Translation "112:124=168:191"
Health 500000
PainChance 255
Mass 25
Radius 20
+PUSHABLE
states
  {
  See:
    BAR1 A 6
    BAR1 B 6 Bright
    Loop
  Pain:
    BEXP A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", TRUE)  
    BEXP A 3 Bright
    BEXP B 3 Bright A_Scream
    BEXP C 3 Bright
    BEXP D 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("TAT__TkExplosion",32)
    BEXP E 6 Bright
    BEXP DCBA 3 Bright
    BEXP A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", FALSE) 
    Goto See
  Death:
    BEXP ABCDE 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("TAT__TkExplosion",32)
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR TAT__TkExplosion : Rocket
{ 
Speed 0
ReactionTime 1
DamageType "TkExplosion"
states
  {
  Spawn:
    MISL B 1 Bright A_CountDown
	Loop
  Death:
	MISL B 3 Bright A_Explode(100,100,0)
	MISL CD 4 Bright
    Stop
  }
}
